 Ipp - true for pp collision; otherwise polarization
       of individual taus from Z/gamma* is set to 0.0
 Ipp    = 1
 CMSENE - used in PDF calculations; only if Ipp = true
          and only for Z/gamma*
 CMSENE = 13600
 Ipol - relevant for Z/gamma* decays 
 0 - events generated without spin effects                
 1 - events generated with all spin effects               
 2 - events generated with spin correlations and <pol>=0  
 3 - events generated with spin correlations and
     polarization but missing angular dependence of <pol>
 Ipol    = 0
 Ipol - relevant for Z/gamma* decays 
 NOTE: For Ipol=0,1 algorithm is identical.               
       However in user program role of wt need change.    
 nonSM2  = 0
 1/0 extra term in cross section, density matrix on/off   
 nonSMN  = 0
 1/0 extra term in cross section, for shapes only? on/off 
 note KEY - for options of matrix elements calculations   
            in cases of final states  with two jets
